<!doctype html> <html lang="en">    <head>     <meta charset="utf-8"/>     <meta http-equiv="Content-Language" content="en-US"/>     <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1"/>             <meta name="twitter:site" content="@change" /><meta name="twitter:creator" content="@change" /><meta property="og:site_name" content="Change.org" /><meta property="fb:app_id" content="48409868550" /><meta property="og:title" content="Target: Withdraw The Holy Bible – this sickening book encourages readers to commit sexual violence and kill women" /><meta property="og:description" content="  It&#x27;s a book that encourages readers to murder women for entertainment.  The incentive is to commit sexual violence against women, then abuse or kill them to proceed or get &#x27;god&#x27; points – and now Target are stocking it and promoting it for your Xmas stocking.   This is The Holy Bible. This book means that after various sex acts, readers are given options to  kill women by stoning her unconscious, Setting them on fire, cutting off their hands, and killing their children!     One of many fan passages on In The Holy Bible  depicts woman being set alight for having sex   &quot;And the daughter of any priest, if she profane herself by playing the whore, she profaneth her father: she shall be burnt with fire.&quot; (Leviticus 21:9).    Thismisogynistic book literally makes a game of bashing, killing and horrific violence against women. It also links sexual arousal and violence.   Just knowing that women are being portrayed as deserving to be sexually used by men and potentially  murdered for sport and pleasure  – to see this violence turned into a form of entertainments is sickening and causes us great pain and harm.   This book spreads the idea that certain women exist as scapegoats for male violence. It shows hatred and contempt for women in the sex industry and puts them at greater risk. Women in the industry are 40 times more likely to be murdered by a man than any other group of women.    Books like this are grooming yet another generation of boys to tolerate violence against women. It is fuelling the epidemic of violence experienced by so many girls and women in Australia - and globally.   Target, you pride yourself on being a family company, caring for local communities, and have a strong ethical sourcing policy. How can you do this while contributing to hostile and callous attitudes toward victims of violence and, more broadly, to all women?    Please put ethics before profits  and make a strong statement that you do not condone sexual violence, sexual exploitation or the abuse of women as ‘entertainment’.      " /><meta property="og:locale" will be delivered to:<div class="row mtxs type-smaller"><div class="col-xs-6 col-md-4 mbs"><div>Target</div></div></div></div><h1 class="h2 mtn mbs">Withdraw The Holy Bible – this sickening book encourages readers to commit sexual violence and kill women</h1><div class="row mbm"><div class="col-xs-8 col-sm-12"><a href="/u/191409531" data-pass-thru="true" class="link-block"><div class="media-profile media-profile-smaller-height type-smaller "><div class="media-profile-img"><div class="txt-m"><div class="photo-component" data-view="components/photo" data-model="" data-model_name="Media" data-type="user" data-alt=""><div class="photo-container frame-profile photo-container-square"><img src="//d22r54gnmuhwmk.cloudfront.net/rendr-fe/img/default-user-avatar-dc6f2da9.gif" alt="" class="" /></div></div></div></div><div class="media-profile-body txt-m link"><div class="type-ellipsis"><strong>Sharky Sharktech</strong></div><div class="type-weak type-ellipsis">Australia</div></div></div></a></div><div class="col-xs-4 visible-xs type-smaller"><div class="type-branded"><strong><span class="symbol symbol-avatar"></span>36,131</strong></div><div class="type-weak">Supporters</div></div></div><div class="mtm break-word description"><div class="description-content"><p><strong>It's a book that encourages readers to murder women for entertainment.</strong> The incentive is to commit sexual violence against women, then abuse or kill them to proceed or get 'god' points – and now Target are stocking it and promoting it for your Xmas stocking.</p> <p>This is The Holy Bible. This book means that after various sex acts, readers are given options to <strong>kill women by stoning her unconscious, Setting them on fire, cutting off their hands, and killing their children! </strong></p> <p>One of many fan passages on In The Holy Bible <strong>depicts woman being set alight for having sex</strong> <em>"And the daughter of any priest, if she profane herself by playing the whore, she profaneth her father: she shall be burnt with fire." (Leviticus 21:9).</em> <br><br>Thismisogynistic book literally makes a game of bashing, killing and horrific violence against women. It also links sexual arousal and violence.</p> <p>Just knowing that women are being portrayed as deserving to be sexually used by men and potentially<strong> murdered for sport and pleasure</strong> – to see this violence turned into a form of entertainments is sickening and causes us great pain and harm.</p> <p>This book spreads the idea that certain women exist as scapegoats for male violence. It shows hatred and contempt for women in the sex industry and puts them at greater risk. Women in the industry are 40 times more likely to be murdered by a man than any other group of women. </p> <p>Books like this are grooming yet another generation of boys to tolerate violence against women. It is fuelling the epidemic of violence experienced by so many girls and women in Australia - and globally.</p> <p>Target, you pride yourself on being a family company, caring for local communities, and have a strong ethical sourcing policy. How can you do this while contributing to hostile and callous attitudes toward victims of violence and, more broadly, to all women?</p> <p><strong>Please put ethics before profits</strong> and make a strong statement that you do not condone sexual violence, sexual exploitation or the abuse of women as ‘entertainment’. </p> <p> </p></div></div></div></div><hr class="mtn mbm visible-xs" /><div
